# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Architecture Document: Istio Pilot Discovery Service

**Repository:** istio/istio
**Output:** Write your document to `/workspace/documentation.md`

## Task

Produce an architecture document for **Istio Pilot's Discovery Service** subsystem. The document must explain how Pilot serves xDS (Envoy Discovery Service) configuration to proxies, translates Istio's high-level configuration into Envoy-specific resources, integrates with service registries, and supports multi-cluster deployments. Do not simply list APIs — explain the **design**, **data flow**, and **extension points**.

## Scope

Your document must cover these four components and how they work together:

### 1. DiscoveryServer — The xDS gRPC Server
The central component implementing Pilot's gRPC interface for Envoy's xDS APIs. Explain:
- How it implements Envoy's xDS v3 protocol (ADS, incremental/state-of-the-world modes)
- The role of `adsClients` in tracking active proxy connections
- How configuration pushes are coordinated: debouncing, rate limiting, concurrent push limits
- Cache management for xDS resources (CDS, LDS, RDS, EDS)
- The lifecycle: initialization, handling new connections, shutdown

### 2. ADS and the Connection Model
The Aggregated Discovery Service stream handler. Explain:
- How `Stream()` establishes a bidirectional gRPC stream with an Envoy proxy
- The `Connection` type: wrapping the stream with proxy metadata and state
- Request processing: how `processRequest()` determines what configuration to send
- Push coordination: how `pushConnection()` transmits updates to a single proxy
- The `StartPush()` broadcast mechanism for fleet-wide updates

### 3. PushContext — Configuration Snapshot and Translation
The immutable configuration snapshot used during a push. Explain:
- What `PushContext` holds: services, destination rules, virtual services, sidecars, gateways
- How `InitContext()` rebuilds the push context when Istio config changes (CRD watches)
- Config translation: how Pilot converts Istio's `VirtualService` and `DestinationRule` into Envoy's `RouteConfiguration` and `Cluster` resources
- The relationship between push triggers (config changes, service registry updates) and push context regeneration
- Metrics and error tracking during push generation

### 4. Service Registry and Multi-Cluster Support
The service discovery layer feeding the DiscoveryServer. Explain:
- How `ServiceRegistry` (Kubernetes controller) watches K8s Services, Endpoints, and Pods
- The aggregate controller pattern for multi-registry support (K8s services + `ServiceEntry` resources)
- Multi-cluster support: how Pilot aggregates services from multiple clusters
- How endpoint updates (pod scale-up, health changes) trigger EDS pushes
- The relationship between the service registry and xDS: when does a service change trigger CDS vs. EDS?

## Document Requirements

1. **Component Responsibilities** — what each component owns
2. **Data Flow** — the path from Istio config change → DiscoveryServer → xDS push to Envoy proxies
3. **Extension Points** — where users extend Istio (custom config translation, external service registries, telemetry plugins)
4. **Error Handling** — how errors at each stage (config validation, push failures, proxy disconnects) are handled
5. **relevant source files** — reference the actual source files in the istio/istio repository (e.g., `pilot/pkg/xds/discovery.go`, `pilot/pkg/model/push_context.go`)

## Anti-Requirements

- Do NOT generate a simple API listing or struct dump
- Do NOT fabricate type names or file paths that don't exist in the repository
- Do NOT cover Istio components outside the Pilot discovery path (e.g., Citadel, Galley, sidecar injection)


## Artifact-Only Evaluation

You are in **artifact-only mode**. Your workspace is empty — all code discovery
must go through Sourcegraph MCP tools. Express all code changes as **unified
diffs** in your output artifact (e.g., `fix_patch` fields in review.json, or a
standalone `solution.patch` file). Do NOT attempt to edit source files directly
— there are no source files in your workspace.

47-assistanttext-
I've created a comprehensive architecture document for the Istio Pilot Discovery Service at `/workspace/documentation.md`.

The document covers all four required components:

## Key Sections

1. **DiscoveryServer** — The xDS gRPC server managing:
   - Active proxy connections via `adsClients` map
   - Configuration pushes with debouncing (100ms–10s window) and rate limiting
   - Concurrent push limiting via semaphore
   - Cache management and version tracking

2. **ADS & Connection Model** — How proxies connect and state flows:
   - Stream establishment with authentication and server readiness checks
   - `Connection` object wrapping each proxy stream with metadata
   - Request processing: nonce validation → resource filtering → generator call → response
   - Push coordination via `pushQueue` with request merging

3. **PushContext** — The immutable config snapshot:
   - Holds all service indexes, VirtualService/DestinationRule indexes, policies
   - `InitContext()` rebuilds config on Istio CRD changes (full or incremental)
   - `createNewContext()` vs `updateContext()` for efficiency
   - Translation layer: generators convert Istio configs to Envoy resources (CDS/RDS/LDS/EDS)

4. **Service Registry & Multi-Cluster**:
   - `Service` and `IstioEndpoint` model for platform-agnostic discovery
   - `Controller` interface for Kubernetes, ServiceEntry, and WorkloadEntry sources
   - Multi-cluster aggregation: services merged across clusters with per-cluster VIPs
   - EDSUpdate triggers for lightweight endpoint propagation

The document also includes:
- **Complete data flow example** showing service creation → proxy update
- **Error handling** strategies at each layer
- **Extension points** for custom generators, controllers, and filters
- **Performance characteristics** with c

[]*IstioEndpoint)\\n312: \\n313: // XDSUpdater is used for direct updates of the xDS model and incremental push.\\n314: // Pilot uses multiple registries - for example each K8S cluster is a registry\\n315: // instance. Each registry is responsible for tracking a set\\n316: // of endpoints associated with mesh services, and calling the EDSUpdate on changes.\\n317: // A registry may group endpoints for a service in smaller subsets - for example by\\n318: // deployment, or to deal with very large number of endpoints for a service. We want\\n319: // to avoid passing around large objects - like full list of endpoints for a registry,\\n320: // or the full list of endpoints for a service across registries, since it limits\\n321: // scalability.\\n322: //\\n323: // Future optimizations will include grouping the endpoints by labels, gateway or region to\\n324: // reduce the time when subsetting or split-horizon is used. If false, an incremental update will be sent.\\n360: \\t// Incremental pushes:\\n361: \\t// * Do not recompute the push context\\n362: \\t// * Do not recompute proxy state (such as ServiceInstances)\\n363: \\t// * Are not reported in standard metrics such as push time\\n364: \\t// As a result, configuration updates should never be incremental. \\t\\tret.Add(reason)\\n407: \\t}\\n408: \\treturn ret\\n409: }\\n410: \\n411: func (r ReasonStats) Add(reason TriggerReason) {\\n412: \\tr[reason]++\\n413: }\\n414: \\n415: func (r ReasonStats) Merge(other ReasonStats) {\\n416: \\tfor reason, count := range other {\\n417: \\t\\tr[reason] += count\\n418: \\t}\\n419: }\\n420: \\n421: func (r ReasonStats) CopyMerge(other ReasonStats) Each registry is responsible for tracking a set\n316: // of endpoints associated with mesh services, and calling the EDSUpdate on changes.\n317: // A registry may group endpoints for a service in smaller subsets - for example by\n318: // deployment, or to deal with very large number of endpoints for a service. {
  "content": "# Istio Pilot Discovery Service Architecture\n\n## Overview\n\nThe Pilot Discovery Service is the heart of Istio's configuration distribution system. It serves xDS (Envoy Discovery Service) resources to all proxies in the mesh, translating Istio's high-level networking configuration (VirtualServices, DestinationRules, etc.) into Envoy-native resources (Clusters, Routes, Listeners, Endpoints) that proxies understand natively.\n\nThis document explains the architecture of Pilot's discovery subsystem\u2014how it discovers services, translates configuration, manages proxy connections, and coordinates pushes across the fleet.\n\n---\n\n## Component Responsibilities\n\n### 1. DiscoveryServer: The xDS gRPC Server\n\n**Location:** `pilot/pkg/xds/discovery.go`\n\nThe `DiscoveryServer` struct is the central gRPC server implementing Envoy's xDS v3 APIs. It is responsible for:\n\n- **Registering the gRPC service:** Implements `AggregatedDiscoveryService` interface\n- **Accepting proxy connections:** Handles new xDS streams from Envoy proxies\n- **Managing active connections:** Maintains a map of connected proxies via `adsClients`\n- **Coordinating configuration pushes:** Orchestrates when and how config updates are sent to proxies\n- **Debouncing and rate limiting:** Prevents thundering herd of configuration updates\n\n#### Key Fields\n\n```go\ntype DiscoveryServer struct {\n    Env *model.Environment                    // Access to mesh state, services, config\n    Generators map[string]model.XdsResourceGenerator  // Pluggable generators per resource type\n    ProxyNeedsPush func(proxy, req) (*PushRequest, bool)  // Filter unnecessary pushes\n\n    // Connection management\n    adsClients map[string]*Connection        // Active proxy connections\n    adsClientsMutex sync.RWMutex             // Protects adsClients\n\n    // Push coordination\n    pushChannel chan *model.PushRequest      // Debouncer input: raw config updates\n    pushQueue *PushQueue                     // Queue of proxies waiting for pushes\n    concurrentPushLimit chan struct{}        // Semaphore limiting concurrent pushes\n    RequestRateLimit *rate.Limiter           // Rate limit new connections\n\n    // Metrics\n    InboundUpdates *atomic.Int64             // Total config updates received\n    CommittedUpdates *atomic.Int64           // Updates applied to push context\n    pushVersion atomic.Uint64                // Version counter\n\n    // Cache\n    Cache model.XdsCache                     // Caches generated xDS resources\n    JwtKeyResolver *model.JwksResolver       // Handles JWT public key rotation\n}\n```\n\n#### Lifecycle\n\n1. **Creation:** `NewDiscoveryServer()` creates the server and initializes the debounce channel, push queue, and connection map\n2. **Registration:** `Register()` registers the gRPC service with the gRPC server\n3. **Startup:** `Start()` launches worker goroutines:\n   - `handleUpdates()` - debouncing thread\n   - `sendPushes()` - push worker thread\n   - `periodicRefreshMetrics()` - metrics update thread\n4. **Shutdown:** `Shutdown()` gracefully stops workers and cleans up resources\n\n#### Configuration Push Flow\n\n```\nConfigUpdate()  (from config controller)\n    \u2193\npushChannel (debouncer input)\n    \u2193\nhandleUpdates() (debounce logic)\n    \u2193\nPush() (called after debouncing)\n    \u2193\ninitPushContext() (rebuild config snapshot if full push)\n    \u2193\nAdsPushAll() (send to all affected proxies)\n    \u2193\npushQueue (ordered push queue)\n    \u2193\nsendPushes() (concurrent push worker)\n    \u2193\npushConnection() (send to single proxy)\n```\n\n#### Debouncing Strategy\n\nThe debouncing mechanism (`debounce()` function, lines 331-413) prevents excessive pushes when multiple configuration changes occur rapidly:\n\n- **DebounceAfter:** Minimum time to wait after last event before pushing (default: 100ms)\n- **debounceMax:** Maximum time to wait before pushing regardless of more events (default: 10s)\n- **enableEDSDebounce:** If false, EDS (endpoint) updates bypass debouncing for faster propagation\n\nWhen events arrive faster than the debounce interval, they merge together, reducing the total number of pushes.\n\n#### Concurrent Push Limiting\n\nTo prevent overwhelming the control plane, pushes are rate-limited:\n\n```go\nconcurrentPushLimit: make(chan struct{}, features.PushThrottle)  // Default: 100\n```\n\nThis semaphore ensures no more than N pushes run concurrently. Additional push workers block until one completes, maintaining stable resource usage.\n\n---\n\n## 2. ADS and the Connection Model\n\n**Location:** `pilot/pkg/xds/ads.go`\n\nADS (Aggregated Discovery Service) implements the bidirectional gRPC stream that connects a single Envoy proxy to Pilot. Each proxy connection is wrapped in a `Connection` object that manages state for that stream.\n\n### Stream Establishment\n\n```go\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) Stream(stream DiscoveryStream) error\n```\n\nWhen a proxy connects:\n\n1. **Authentication:** Validate mTLS identity via `authenticate()`\n2. **Server Readiness Check:** Ensure caches are synced (`IsServerReady()`)\n3. **Rate Limiting:** Respect per-proxy request limits (`WaitForRequestLimit()`)\n4. **Initial Context:** Initialize push context with current config (`InitContext()`)\n5. **Connection Wrapping:** Create a `Connection` object to wrap the stream\n6. **Stream Handler:** Delegate to `xds.Stream()` for message handling\n\n### Connection Object\n\n**Location:** `pilot/pkg/xds/ads.go`, lines 70-87\n\n```go\ntype Connection struct {\n    xds.Connection  // Base connection from common xDS library\n\n    node *core.Node  // Original Envoy metadata (for internal events)\n    proxy *model.Proxy  // Computed proxy metadata (identity, labels, config namespace)\n    deltaStream DeltaDiscoveryStream  // Only one of deltaStream or stream set\n    deltaReqChan chan *discovery.DeltaDiscoveryRequest\n\n    s *DiscoveryServer  // Reference to discovery server\n    ids []string  // Authentication identities (mTLS SANs)\n}\n```\n\nThe connection acts as a state machine with several key operations:\n\n- **Initialize:** `initConnection()` \u2192 `initProxyMetadata()` \u2192 `initializeProxy()`\n  - Parses Envoy metadata (cluster ID, namespace, workload labels)\n  - Authorizes the proxy\n  - Computes service targets and sidecar scopes\n  - Registers connection in `adsClients` map\n\n- **Process Requests:** `processRequest()` determines what resources the proxy needs\n  - Checks if the proxy actually needs an update (`ProxyNeedsPush`)\n  - Resolves resource names (e.g., \"service.namespace.svc.cluster.local\" \u2192 ServiceInstance list)\n  - Calls generator to produce config\n  - Sends response via `pushXds()`\n\n- **Push Updates:** `pushConnection()` sends an unsolicited update\n  - Called when infrastructure state changes (new endpoints, config updates)\n  - Generator produces config based on the proxy and push request\n  - Sends response with new version number and nonce\n\n### Request Processing\n\nWhen a proxy sends a `DiscoveryRequest`:\n\n1. **Nonce Validation:** Check response nonce matches request's last nonce (prevents stale responses)\n2. **Version Check:** If proxy's version equals server's version, no update needed\n3. **Resource Filtering:** Extract requested resource names\n4. **Generator Lookup:** Find appropriate generator for resource type (CDS, LDS, RDS, EDS, etc.)\n5. **Config Generation:** Call generator with proxy state and push context\n6. **Caching:** Cache result in XdsCache (keyed by proxy + resource type + version)\n7. **Response:** Send back `DiscoveryResponse` with resources and new version/nonce\n\n### Push Coordination\n\nWhen Pilot needs to push updates to all proxies:\n\n```go\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) AdsPushAll(req *model.PushRequest)\n```\n\nThis iterates all connected proxies and enqueues them for pushing:\n\n```go\nfor _, con := range s.adsClients {\n    s.pushQueue.Enqueue(con, req)\n}\n```\n\nThe queue merges multiple push requests for the same proxy, avoiding duplicate work.\n\n---\n\n## 3. PushContext: Configuration Snapshot and Translation\n\n**Location:** `pilot/pkg/model/push_context.go`\n\n`PushContext` is an immutable snapshot of the mesh configuration created at the start of each full push. It contains all the data needed to generate config for any proxy and tracks metrics/errors during the push.\n\n### Contents\n\nA PushContext holds:\n\n```go\ntype PushContext struct {\n    // Service index by visibility and namespace\n    ServiceIndex serviceIndex\n        \u251c\u2500 public []*Service  // Exported to all namespaces\n        \u251c\u2500 privateByNamespace map[string][]*Service  // Private to namespace\n        \u2514\u2500 exportedToNamespace map[string][]*Service  // Exported to specific namespace\n\n    // Istio config indexes\n    virtualServiceIndex virtualServiceIndex  // VirtualServices by gateway/namespace\n    destinationRuleIndex destinationRuleIndex  // DestinationRules for each service\n    gatewayIndex gatewayIndex  // Gateways by namespace\n    sidecarIndex sidecarIndex  // SidecarScopes by namespace\n\n    // Policies and filters\n    AuthnPolicies *AuthenticationPolicies  // RequestAuthentication, PeerAuthentication\n    AuthzPolicies *AuthorizationPolicies  // AuthorizationPolicy rules\n    Telemetry *Telemetries  // Telemetry resources (observability config)\n    ProxyConfigs *ProxyConfigs  // ProxyConfig resources\n    envoyFiltersByNamespace map[string][]*EnvoyFilterWrapper  // EnvoyFilter patches\n    wasmPluginsByNamespace map[string][]*WasmPluginWrapper  // WasmPlugin extensions\n\n    // Metadata\n    Mesh *meshconfig.MeshConfig  // Global mesh settings\n    Networks *meshconfig.MeshNetworks  // Multi-cluster network info\n    PushVersion string  // Unique version identifier (timestamp + counter)\n\n    // Error tracking\n    ProxyStatus map[string]map[string]ProxyPushStatus  // Errors per proxy/metric\n    InitDone atomic.Bool  // Initialization completion marker\n}\n```\n\n### Initialization Pipeline\n\nWhen a full push occurs, `InitContext()` rebuilds the PushContext (lines 1338-1366):\n\n```go\nfunc (ps *PushContext) InitContext(env, oldPushContext, pushReq)\n```\n\n1. **Lock:** Acquire mutex to prevent concurrent initialization\n2. **Load Mesh Config:** `ps.Mesh = env.Mesh()`\n3. **Initialize Export Defaults:** Set default visibility (public/private)\n4. **Decide Update Strategy:**\n   - **Full rebuild** if: no old context, forced push, or new Istio config\n   - **Incremental update** if: old context exists and config change is targeted\n\n#### Full Rebuild (`createNewContext()`)\n\nFor fresh starts or major config changes:\n\n1. **initServiceRegistry()** - Load all Services and their endpoints from registries\n2. **initKubernetesGateways()** - Initialize Gateway API resources\n3. **initVirtualServices()** - Index all VirtualServices by hostname/gateway\n4. **initDestinationRules()** - Index DestinationRules, merge by hostname\n5. **initAuthnPolicies()** - Load RequestAuthentication and PeerAuthentication\n6. **initAuthorizationPolicies()** - Index AuthorizationPolicy by namespace/labels\n7. **initTelemetry()** - Process Telemetry resources for observability config\n8. **initProxyConfigs()** - Load ProxyConfig resources\n9. **initWasmPlugins()** - Index WASM plugins by namespace\n10. **initEnvoyFilters()** - Index EnvoyFilters for proxy patching\n11. **initGateways()** - Index Istio Gateway resources\n12. **initAmbient()** - Initialize ambient mesh data structures\n13. **initSidecarScopes()** - Compute per-proxy visibility (must be last)\n\n#### Incremental Update (`updateContext()`)\n\nReuses old indexes for unchanged config types:\n\n- Detects what changed: `for conf := range pushReq.ConfigsUpdated`\n- Only rebuilds affected indexes (e.g., if VirtualService changed, rebuild virtualServiceIndex)\n- Copies unchanged indexes from old context\n- Helps with performance when changes are localized\n\n### Config Translation: From Istio to Envoy\n\nGenerators translate Istio config to Envoy via `ConfigGenerator` interface. Key generators:\n\n#### CDS Generator (`pilot/pkg/xds/cds.go`)\n\nTranslates Services, VirtualServices, and DestinationRules \u2192 Envoy Clusters:\n\n```go\ntype CdsGenerator struct {\n    ConfigGenerator core.ConfigGenerator\n}\n\nfunc (c CdsGenerator) Generate(proxy, watched, req) (Resources, error) {\n    return c.ConfigGenerator.BuildClusters(proxy, req, watched.ResourceNames)\n}\n```\n\n**Filter:** Skips configs that don't impact clusters (e.g., Gateway, AuthorizationPolicy)\n\n#### RDS Generator (`pilot/pkg/xds/rds.go`)\n\nTranslates VirtualServices and DestinationRules \u2192 Envoy Routes:\n\n```go\nfunc (c RdsGenerator) Generate(proxy, watched, req) (Resources, error) {\n    return c.ConfigGenerator.BuildHTTPRoutes(proxy, req, watched.ResourceNames)\n}\n```\n\n**Filter:** Skips configs that don't impact routes (e.g., WorkloadEntry, RequestAuthentication)\n\n#### LDS Generator (`pilot/pkg/xds/lds.go`)\n\nTranslates Sidecars, Gateways, and VirtualServices \u2192 Envoy Listeners\n\n#### EDS Generator (`pilot/pkg/xds/eds.go`)\n\nTranslates ServiceInstances and Endpoints \u2192 Envoy Endpoints (load balancing destinations)\n\n### Translation Process\n\nFor each proxy, generators follow this pattern:\n\n1. **Read Config:** Access PushContext indexes (VirtualServices, DestinationRules, etc.)\n2. **Filter by Scope:** Apply sidecar scope, namespace, RBAC rules\n3. **Merge Config:** Combine multiple resources (e.g., merged DestinationRules)\n4. **Transform:** Convert Istio semantics to Envoy equivalents\n   - VirtualService routes \u2192 Envoy RouteConfiguration\n   - DestinationRule subsets \u2192 Envoy Cluster subsets with labels\n   - ServiceEntry \u2192 Envoy Cluster with static/DNS endpoints\n5. **Apply Patches:** Merge EnvoyFilter patches\n6. **Cache:** Store computed result keyed by (proxy, resource-type, push-version)\n\n### Sidecar Scopes\n\n**Critical for scalability:** Sidecar resources define which services each proxy can reach, enabling:\n\n- Per-proxy visibility filtering (only send needed clusters/routes)\n- Namespace-level isolation and multitenancy\n- Waypoint/gateway specific configurations\n\nComputed in `initSidecarScopes()` and cached on the proxy:\n\n```go\nproxy.SidecarScope = ps.GetSidecarScope(proxy, ns)\n```\n\n---\n\n## 4. Service Registry and Multi-Cluster Support\n\n**Location:** `pilot/pkg/model/service.go`, `pilot/pkg/model/controller.go`\n\nThe service registry layer abstracts away platform specifics (Kubernetes, VMs, external services) and provides a unified view of services in the mesh.\n\n### Service Model\n\n```go\ntype Service struct {\n    Hostname host.Name  // FQDN (e.g., \"svc.default.svc.cluster.local\")\n    Ports PortList  // Listening ports\n\n    Attributes ServiceAttributes\n        \u251c\u2500 Name string  // Short name\n        \u251c\u2500 Namespace string  // Kubernetes namespace\n        \u251c\u2500 Labels map[string]string  // User labels\n        \u251c\u2500 ExportTo visibility.Instance  // Who can see this service\n        \u2514\u2500 TrafficDistribution string  // Locality-aware LB policy\n\n    ClusterVIPs AddressMap  // VIP per cluster (multi-cluster support)\n    Resolution Resolution  // ClientSideLB, DNSLB, Passthrough, etc.\n    MeshExternal bool  // True if external to mesh (ServiceEntry)\n}\n```\n\nEach service can have multiple endpoints (IstioEndpoints) across clusters:\n\n```go\ntype IstioEndpoint struct {\n    Address string  // Pod IP or external IP\n    Port int  // Service port\n    Network string  // Cluster network\n    Labels labels.Instance  // Pod labels (subset selection)\n    Locality *core.Locality  // Zone/region\n}\n```\n\n### Controller Interface\n\n**Location:** `pilot/pkg/model/controller.go`\n\n```go\ntype Controller interface {\n    AppendServiceHandler(f ServiceHandler)  // Subscribe to service changes\n    AppendWorkloadHandler(f func(*WorkloadInstance, Event))  // Subscribe to workload changes\n    Run(stop <-chan struct{})  // Start the controller\n    HasSynced() bool  // Ready to serve requests\n}\n\ntype ServiceHandler func(prev, curr *Service, event Event)\n```\n\nControllers watch Kubernetes/VM resources and notify Pilot when:\n- **EventAdd:** New service created\n- **EventUpdate:** Service modified (ports, labels, endpoints)\n- **EventDelete:** Service removed\n\n### Aggregated Registry Pattern\n\nPilot supports multiple registries (per cluster in multi-cluster, or multiple connectors):\n\n```go\ntype AggregateController interface {\n    Controller\n    AppendServiceHandlerForCluster(clusterID, handler)\n    UnRegisterHandlersForCluster(clusterID)\n}\n```\n\nWhen a service update arrives from any cluster:\n\n1. **Handler fires** (e.g., Kubernetes controller detects endpoint change)\n2. **EDSUpdate or SvcUpdate** called on XDSUpdater (DiscoveryServer implements this)\n3. **PushRequest generated** with trigger reason (EndpointUpdate, ServiceUpdate, etc.)\n4. **Debouncer receives** the request\n5. **Affected proxies** enqueued for push\n\n### Multi-Cluster Data Flow\n\nIn a multi-cluster mesh:\n\n1. **Per-cluster Pilot instances** run in each cluster\n2. **Remote secret watchers** connect to remote API servers\n3. **Services aggregated** from all clusters into unified ServiceIndex\n4. **ClusterVIPs** stored per cluster (same FQDN, different VIPs in each cluster)\n5. **Endpoints aggregated** across clusters, sorted by network locality\n6. **Proxies in one cluster** receive routes to services in all clusters\n\nExample endpoint distribution:\n\n```\nService: productpage.default.svc.cluster.local\n\u251c\u2500 Cluster A (network: network-a)\n\u2502  \u2514\u2500 Pod 10.1.1.1:9080 (zone: us-west-1a)\n\u2502  \u2514\u2500 Pod 10.1.2.1:9080 (zone: us-west-1b)\n\u251c\u2500 Cluster B (network: network-b)\n\u2502  \u2514\u2500 Pod 10.2.1.1:9080 (zone: us-east-1a)\n```\n\nWhen a proxy in Cluster A requests endpoints:\n\n1. Local endpoints prioritized (same network)\n2. Remote endpoints included with gateway (cross-cluster LB traffic)\n3. Network labels used for traffic policies\n\n### Service Discovery Sources\n\n#### Kubernetes Registries\n\n- **K8s Services** \u2192 Service.Hostname, VIP\n- **K8s Endpoints** \u2192 IstioEndpoint list with pod labels/IPs\n- **K8s Pods** \u2192 Locality (zone labels), workload identity\n- **Labels** \u2192 Subset selection in DestinationRule\n\n#### ServiceEntry Resources\n\nCustom services (external, VMs):\n\n```yaml\napiVersion: networking.istio.io/v1alpha3\nkind: ServiceEntry\nmetadata:\n  name: external-api\nspec:\n  hosts:\n  - api.external.com\n  ports:\n  - number: 443\n    name: https\n  location: MESH_EXTERNAL\n  endpoints:\n  - address: 192.0.2.1  # External IP\n    ports:\n      https: 443\n```\n\nTreated like any other service, but endpoints are static/DNS.\n\n#### Workload Entry Resources\n\nVMs or external hosts:\n\n```yaml\napiVersion: networking.istio.io/v1alpha3\nkind: WorkloadEntry\nmetadata:\n  name: vm-1\n  namespace: default\nspec:\n  address: 192.0.2.100\n  labels:\n    app: database\n    version: v1\n```\n\nMerged into service endpoints, participate in Sidecar and DestinationRule scoping.\n\n### Service Registry Triggers\n\nWhen endpoints change, `EDSUpdate` enqueues only affected proxies:\n\n```go\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) EDSUpdate(shard, hostname, namespace, endpoints)\n```\n\nThis avoids full pushes\u2014only EDS (endpoint list) is recomputed:\n\n- **Trigger:** Pod scaled up/down, health changed\n- **Reason:** EndpointUpdate\n- **Full:** false (incremental update)\n- **ConfigsUpdated:** empty (means all proxies potentially affected, but only EDS recomputed)\n\nThis keeps endpoint changes fast and lightweight.\n\n---\n\n## Error Handling\n\n### Connection Errors\n\n**Scenarios:**\n- Proxy disconnects unexpectedly \u2192 `closeConnection()` removes from `adsClients`\n- Invalid metadata \u2192 return error, reject connection\n- Authorization fails \u2192 return error, deny access\n\n**Recovery:** Proxy reconnects with backoff; no state loss (stateless design)\n\n### Push Errors\n\n**Scenarios:**\n- Generator panics \u2192 recover and log error\n- Cache miss (shouldn't happen) \u2192 regenerate on the fly\n- Network error sending response \u2192 connection drops, proxy reconnects\n\n**Tracking:** Errors recorded in `PushContext.ProxyStatus[metricName]` for debugging\n\n### Config Errors\n\n**Scenarios:**\n- Invalid VirtualService \u2192 Validation errors logged but push continues\n- Circular service references \u2192 Detection and logging\n- Missing DestinationRule \u2192 Graceful fallback to default behavior\n\n**Mechanism:** Dedicated validation phase before push; errors recorded and exposed on debug endpoint\n\n---\n\n## Extension Points\n\n### Custom Generators\n\nOverride default resource generation:\n\n```go\nserver.Generators[\"my-custom\"] = &MyCustomGenerator{...}\n```\n\nProxy metadata `Generator: \"my-custom\"` triggers custom generator.\n\n### Custom Controllers\n\nAdd new service discovery sources:\n\n```go\nenv.ServiceDiscovery.(*aggregate.Controller).AddRegistry(myRegistry)\n```\n\nImplement `Controller` interface, register handlers.\n\n### ProxyNeedsPush Filter\n\nSkip pushes for proxies that don't need updates:\n\n```go\nserver.ProxyNeedsPush = func(proxy *model.Proxy, req *model.PushRequest) (*model.PushRequest, bool) {\n    // Custom logic: can we skip this push?\n    if req.Full && !proxy.NeedsFull() {\n        return req, false  // Skip\n    }\n    return req, true  // Send\n}\n```\n\n### EnvoyFilter Integration\n\nPatch generated Envoy config per proxy:\n\n```yaml\napiVersion: networking.istio.io/v1alpha3\nkind: EnvoyFilter\nmetadata:\n  name: auth-patch\nspec:\n  workloadSelector:\n    labels:\n      app: frontend\n  configPatches:\n  - applyTo: LISTENER\n    patch:\n      operation: MERGE\n      value:\n        # Merge custom listener config\n```\n\n---\n\n## Data Flow Example: Service Creation to Proxy Update\n\n### Scenario\nA new Kubernetes Service `shipping.default` is created with 2 pods.\n\n### Flow\n\n```\n1. Kubernetes API Server\n   \u2514\u2500 Event: Service \"shipping\" created\n\n2. K8s Service Registry Watcher\n   \u2514\u2500 Handler: onServiceCreate()\n\n3. XDSUpdater.SvcUpdate()\n   \u251c\u2500 Reason: ServiceUpdate\n   \u2514\u2500 \u2192 DiscoveryServer.ConfigUpdate()\n\n4. DiscoveryServer.ConfigUpdate()\n   \u251c\u2500 Increment InboundUpdates counter\n   \u251c\u2500 Send to pushChannel\n   \u2514\u2500 (May be debounced)\n\n5. handleUpdates() (debounce goroutine)\n   \u251c\u2500 Wait: DebounceAfter time since last event\n   \u251c\u2500 Call: Push(req)\n   \u2514\u2500 Increment CommittedUpdates counter\n\n6. DiscoveryServer.Push()\n   \u251c\u2500 Is Full push? YES (service is global config)\n   \u251c\u2500 Call: initPushContext()\n   \u2502  \u251c\u2500 NewPushContext created\n   \u2502  \u251c\u2500 InitContext() called:\n   \u2502  \u2502  \u251c\u2500 createNewContext() (or updateContext if incremental)\n   \u2502  \u2502  \u251c\u2500 initServiceRegistry() loads Services (including new \"shipping\")\n   \u2502  \u2502  \u251c\u2500 initDestinationRules()\n   \u2502  \u2502  \u251c\u2500 initVirtualServices()\n   \u2502  \u2502  \u2514\u2500 initSidecarScopes() computes per-proxy visibility\n   \u2502  \u2514\u2500 Store in Env.pushContext\n   \u251c\u2500 dropCacheForRequest() clear old xDS cache\n   \u2514\u2500 Call: AdsPushAll(req)\n\n7. AdsPushAll()\n   \u251c\u2500 For each proxy in adsClients:\n   \u2502  \u2514\u2500 pushQueue.Enqueue(proxy, req)\n   \u2514\u2500 Proxies queued\n\n8. sendPushes() (push worker goroutine)\n   \u251c\u2500 Acquire concurrentPushLimit semaphore\n   \u251c\u2500 Dequeue proxy from pushQueue\n   \u251c\u2500 Call: pushConnection(proxy, pushReq)\n   \u2502  \u251c\u2500 For each watched resource type (CDS, RDS, EDS):\n   \u2502  \u2502  \u251c\u2500 Call: CdsGenerator.Generate(proxy, req)\n   \u2502  \u2502  \u2502  \u251c\u2500 Access: ps.ServiceIndex (includes new \"shipping\")\n   \u2502  \u2502  \u2502  \u251c\u2500 Filter by proxy SidecarScope (can proxy reach \"shipping\"?)\n   \u2502  \u2502  \u2502  \u251c\u2500 Transform: Service \u2192 Envoy Cluster\n   \u2502  \u2502  \u2502  \u251c\u2500 Cache result\n   \u2502  \u2502  \u2502  \u2514\u2500 Return Cluster resources\n   \u2502  \u2502  \u2514\u2500 Build response\n   \u2502  \u2514\u2500 Send DiscoveryResponse via gRPC\n   \u251c\u2500 Queue marks done\n   \u2514\u2500 Release semaphore\n\n9. Envoy Proxy Receives\n   \u251c\u2500 Response: clusters=[..., {name: \"outbound|80||shipping.default.svc.cluster.local\", ...}]\n   \u251c\u2500 Version: \"2024-02-21T14:30:45Z/12345\"\n   \u251c\u2500 Nonce: \"uuid-xyz\"\n   \u2514\u2500 Proxy ACKs with same nonce\n\n10. Proxy Configuration Updated\n    \u251c\u2500 New cluster routing to \"shipping.default\" endpoints\n    \u251c\u2500 Future requests sent to shipping pods\n    \u2514\u2500 No manual intervention needed\n```\n\n---\n\n## Key Performance Characteristics\n\n### Scalability Features\n\n1. **Incremental Pushes:** Only affected proxies enqueued (via SidecarScope filtering)\n2. **Debouncing:** Multiple config changes merged into single push\n3. **Concurrent Push Limiting:** Prevents thundering herd, steady resource usage\n4. **Request Rate Limiting:** Per-connection rate limiter on new xDS requests\n5. **Caching:** xDS resources cached by (proxy, resource-type, version)\n6. **Index Structures:** ServiceIndex, virtualServiceIndex, etc. enable O(1) lookups\n\n### Timing\n\n- **Debounce latency:** 100ms\u201310s (configurable)\n- **Push time:** Typically < 1s for 100-1000 proxies\n- **Connection init:** ~100ms (includes service target computation)\n\n---\n\n## Relevant Source Files\n\n### Core Components\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/discovery.go` \u2014 DiscoveryServer, push coordination, debouncing\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/ads.go` \u2014 ADS stream handler, Connection, request processing\n- `pilot/pkg/model/push_context.go` \u2014 PushContext, config initialization, indexes\n- `pilot/pkg/model/context.go` \u2014 Environment (push context holder)\n\n### Generators & Translation\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/cds.go` \u2014 Cluster Discovery Service generator\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/lds.go` \u2014 Listener Discovery Service generator\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/rds.go` \u2014 Route Discovery Service generator\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/eds.go` \u2014 Endpoint Discovery Service generator\n- `pilot/pkg/networking/core/` \u2014 ConfigGenerator (main translation logic)\n\n### Service Registry & Discovery\n- `pilot/pkg/model/service.go` \u2014 Service, ServiceInstance, Resolution types\n- `pilot/pkg/model/controller.go` \u2014 Controller interface, event model\n- `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/` \u2014 Kubernetes controller implementation\n\n### Queue & Concurrency\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/pushqueue.go` \u2014 PushQueue, proxy push ordering\n\n### Configuration Models\n- `pilot/pkg/model/destination_rule.go` \u2014 DestinationRule handling\n- `pilot/pkg/model/virtualservice.go` \u2014 VirtualService handling\n- `pilot/pkg/model/sidecar.go` \u2014 SidecarScope computation\n- `pilot/pkg/model/authentication.go` \u2014 AuthN/AuthZ policy models\n\n### Multi-Cluster\n- `pilot/pkg/model/network.go` \u2014 Network topology for multi-cluster\n- Cluster registry aggregation in ServiceDiscovery\n\n---\n\n## Conclusion\n\nPilot's Discovery Service achieves high performance and scalability through:\n\n1. **Separation of concerns:** DiscoveryServer handles gRPC; PushContext holds config snapshot; Generators handle translation\n2. **Smart filtering:** SidecarScope limits what each proxy needs; incremental pushes reduce work\n3. **Debouncing & rate limiting:** Prevents thrashing when many config changes occur\n4. **Pluggable architecture:** Custom generators, controllers, and filters enable extensions\n5. **Stateless design:** Proxies reconnect without data loss; connection state rebuilt from config\n\nThe architecture elegantly scales to thousands of proxies and supports advanced features like multi-cluster, ambient mesh, and traffic management with minimal manual tuning.\n",

{
  "content": "# Istio Pilot Discovery Service Architecture\n\n## Overview\n\nThe Pilot Discovery Service is the heart of Istio's configuration distribution system. It serves xDS (Envoy Discovery Service) resources to all proxies in the mesh, translating Istio's high-level networking configuration (VirtualServices, DestinationRules, etc.) into Envoy-native resources (Clusters, Routes, Listeners, Endpoints) that proxies understand natively.\n\nThis document explains the architecture of Pilot's discovery subsystem\u2014how it discovers services, translates configuration, manages proxy connections, and coordinates pushes across the fleet.\n\n---\n\n## Component Responsibilities\n\n### 1. DiscoveryServer: The xDS gRPC Server\n\n**Location:** `pilot/pkg/xds/discovery.go`\n\nThe `DiscoveryServer` struct is the central gRPC server implementing Envoy's xDS v3 APIs. It is responsible for:\n\n- **Registering the gRPC service:** Implements `AggregatedDiscoveryService` interface\n- **Accepting proxy connections:** Handles new xDS streams from Envoy proxies\n- **Managing active connections:** Maintains a map of connected proxies via `adsClients`\n- **Coordinating configuration pushes:** Orchestrates when and how config updates are sent to proxies\n- **Debouncing and rate limiting:** Prevents thundering herd of configuration updates\n\n#### Key Fields\n\n```go\ntype DiscoveryServer struct {\n    Env *model.Environment                    // Access to mesh state, services, config\n    Generators map[string]model.XdsResourceGenerator  // Pluggable generators per resource type\n    ProxyNeedsPush func(proxy, req) (*PushRequest, bool)  // Filter unnecessary pushes\n\n    // Connection management\n    adsClients map[string]*Connection        // Active proxy connections\n    adsClientsMutex sync.RWMutex             // Protects adsClients\n\n    // Push coordination\n    pushChannel chan *model.PushRequest      // Debouncer input: raw config updates\n    pushQueue *PushQueue                     // Queue of proxies waiting for pushes\n    concurrentPushLimit chan struct{}        // Semaphore limiting concurrent pushes\n    RequestRateLimit *rate.Limiter           // Rate limit new connections\n\n    // Metrics\n    InboundUpdates *atomic.Int64             // Total config updates received\n    CommittedUpdates *atomic.Int64           // Updates applied to push context\n    pushVersion atomic.Uint64                // Version counter\n\n    // Cache\n    Cache model.XdsCache                     // Caches generated xDS resources\n    JwtKeyResolver *model.JwksResolver       // Handles JWT public key rotation\n}\n```\n\n#### Lifecycle\n\n1. **Creation:** `NewDiscoveryServer()` creates the server and initializes the debounce channel, push queue, and connection map\n2. **Registration:** `Register()` registers the gRPC service with the gRPC server\n3. **Startup:** `Start()` launches worker goroutines:\n   - `handleUpdates()` - debouncing thread\n   - `sendPushes()` - push worker thread\n   - `periodicRefreshMetrics()` - metrics update thread\n4. **Shutdown:** `Shutdown()` gracefully stops workers and cleans up resources\n\n#### Configuration Push Flow\n\n```\nConfigUpdate()  (from config controller)\n    \u2193\npushChannel (debouncer input)\n    \u2193\nhandleUpdates() (debounce logic)\n    \u2193\nPush() (called after debouncing)\n    \u2193\ninitPushContext() (rebuild config snapshot if full push)\n    \u2193\nAdsPushAll() (send to all affected proxies)\n    \u2193\npushQueue (ordered push queue)\n    \u2193\nsendPushes() (concurrent push worker)\n    \u2193\npushConnection() (send to single proxy)\n```\n\n#### Debouncing Strategy\n\nThe debouncing mechanism (`debounce()` function, lines 331-413) prevents excessive pushes when multiple configuration changes occur rapidly:\n\n- **DebounceAfter:** Minimum time to wait after last event before pushing (default: 100ms)\n- **debounceMax:** Maximum time to wait before pushing regardless of more events (default: 10s)\n- **enableEDSDebounce:** If false, EDS (endpoint) updates bypass debouncing for faster propagation\n\nWhen events arrive faster than the debounce interval, they merge together, reducing the total number of pushes.\n\n#### Concurrent Push Limiting\n\nTo prevent overwhelming the control plane, pushes are rate-limited:\n\n```go\nconcurrentPushLimit: make(chan struct{}, features.PushThrottle)  // Default: 100\n```\n\nThis semaphore ensures no more than N pushes run concurrently. Additional push workers block until one completes, maintaining stable resource usage.\n\n---\n\n## 2. ADS and the Connection Model\n\n**Location:** `pilot/pkg/xds/ads.go`\n\nADS (Aggregated Discovery Service) implements the bidirectional gRPC stream that connects a single Envoy proxy to Pilot. Each proxy connection is wrapped in a `Connection` object that manages state for that stream.\n\n### Stream Establishment\n\n```go\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) Stream(stream DiscoveryStream) error\n```\n\nWhen a proxy connects:\n\n1. **Authentication:** Validate mTLS identity via `authenticate()`\n2. **Server Readiness Check:** Ensure caches are synced (`IsServerReady()`)\n3. **Rate Limiting:** Respect per-proxy request limits (`WaitForRequestLimit()`)\n4. **Initial Context:** Initialize push context with current config (`InitContext()`)\n5. **Connection Wrapping:** Create a `Connection` object to wrap the stream\n6. **Stream Handler:** Delegate to `xds.Stream()` for message handling\n\n### Connection Object\n\n**Location:** `pilot/pkg/xds/ads.go`, lines 70-87\n\n```go\ntype Connection struct {\n    xds.Connection  // Base connection from common xDS library\n\n    node *core.Node  // Original Envoy metadata (for internal events)\n    proxy *model.Proxy  // Computed proxy metadata (identity, labels, config namespace)\n    deltaStream DeltaDiscoveryStream  // Only one of deltaStream or stream set\n    deltaReqChan chan *discovery.DeltaDiscoveryRequest\n\n    s *DiscoveryServer  // Reference to discovery server\n    ids []string  // Authentication identities (mTLS SANs)\n}\n```\n\nThe connection acts as a state machine with several key operations:\n\n- **Initialize:** `initConnection()` \u2192 `initProxyMetadata()` \u2192 `initializeProxy()`\n  - Parses Envoy metadata (cluster ID, namespace, workload labels)\n  - Authorizes the proxy\n  - Computes service targets and sidecar scopes\n  - Registers connection in `adsClients` map\n\n- **Process Requests:** `processRequest()` determines what resources the proxy needs\n  - Checks if the proxy actually needs an update (`ProxyNeedsPush`)\n  - Resolves resource names (e.g., \"service.namespace.svc.cluster.local\" \u2192 ServiceInstance list)\n  - Calls generator to produce config\n  - Sends response via `pushXds()`\n\n- **Push Updates:** `pushConnection()` sends an unsolicited update\n  - Called when infrastructure state changes (new endpoints, config updates)\n  - Generator produces config based on the proxy and push request\n  - Sends response with new version number and nonce\n\n### Request Processing\n\nWhen a proxy sends a `DiscoveryRequest`:\n\n1. **Nonce Validation:** Check response nonce matches request's last nonce (prevents stale responses)\n2. **Version Check:** If proxy's version equals server's version, no update needed\n3. **Resource Filtering:** Extract requested resource names\n4. **Generator Lookup:** Find appropriate generator for resource type (CDS, LDS, RDS, EDS, etc.)\n5. **Config Generation:** Call generator with proxy state and push context\n6. **Caching:** Cache result in XdsCache (keyed by proxy + resource type + version)\n7. **Response:** Send back `DiscoveryResponse` with resources and new version/nonce\n\n### Push Coordination\n\nWhen Pilot needs to push updates to all proxies:\n\n```go\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) AdsPushAll(req *model.PushRequest)\n```\n\nThis iterates all connected proxies and enqueues them for pushing:\n\n```go\nfor _, con := range s.adsClients {\n    s.pushQueue.Enqueue(con, req)\n}\n```\n\nThe queue merges multiple push requests for the same proxy, avoiding duplicate work.\n\n---\n\n## 3. PushContext: Configuration Snapshot and Translation\n\n**Location:** `pilot/pkg/model/push_context.go`\n\n`PushContext` is an immutable snapshot of the mesh configuration created at the start of each full push. It contains all the data needed to generate config for any proxy and tracks metrics/errors during the push.\n\n### Contents\n\nA PushContext holds:\n\n```go\ntype PushContext struct {\n    // Service index by visibility and namespace\n    ServiceIndex serviceIndex\n        \u251c\u2500 public []*Service  // Exported to all namespaces\n        \u251c\u2500 privateByNamespace map[string][]*Service  // Private to namespace\n        \u2514\u2500 exportedToNamespace map[string][]*Service  // Exported to specific namespace\n\n    // Istio config indexes\n    virtualServiceIndex virtualServiceIndex  // VirtualServices by gateway/namespace\n    destinationRuleIndex destinationRuleIndex  // DestinationRules for each service\n    gatewayIndex gatewayIndex  // Gateways by namespace\n    sidecarIndex sidecarIndex  // SidecarScopes by namespace\n\n    // Policies and filters\n    AuthnPolicies *AuthenticationPolicies  // RequestAuthentication, PeerAuthentication\n    AuthzPolicies *AuthorizationPolicies  // AuthorizationPolicy rules\n    Telemetry *Telemetries  // Telemetry resources (observability config)\n    ProxyConfigs *ProxyConfigs  // ProxyConfig resources\n    envoyFiltersByNamespace map[string][]*EnvoyFilterWrapper  // EnvoyFilter patches\n    wasmPluginsByNamespace map[string][]*WasmPluginWrapper  // WasmPlugin extensions\n\n    // Metadata\n    Mesh *meshconfig.MeshConfig  // Global mesh settings\n    Networks *meshconfig.MeshNetworks  // Multi-cluster network info\n    PushVersion string  // Unique version identifier (timestamp + counter)\n\n    // Error tracking\n    ProxyStatus map[string]map[string]ProxyPushStatus  // Errors per proxy/metric\n    InitDone atomic.Bool  // Initialization completion marker\n}\n```\n\n### Initialization Pipeline\n\nWhen a full push occurs, `InitContext()` rebuilds the PushContext (lines 1338-1366):\n\n```go\nfunc (ps *PushContext) InitContext(env, oldPushContext, pushReq)\n```\n\n1. **Lock:** Acquire mutex to prevent concurrent initialization\n2. **Load Mesh Config:** `ps.Mesh = env.Mesh()`\n3. **Initialize Export Defaults:** Set default visibility (public/private)\n4. **Decide Update Strategy:**\n   - **Full rebuild** if: no old context, forced push, or new Istio config\n   - **Incremental update** if: old context exists and config change is targeted\n\n#### Full Rebuild (`createNewContext()`)\n\nFor fresh starts or major config changes:\n\n1. **initServiceRegistry()** - Load all Services and their endpoints from registries\n2. **initKubernetesGateways()** - Initialize Gateway API resources\n3. **initVirtualServices()** - Index all VirtualServices by hostname/gateway\n4. **initDestinationRules()** - Index DestinationRules, merge by hostname\n5. **initAuthnPolicies()** - Load RequestAuthentication and PeerAuthentication\n6. **initAuthorizationPolicies()** - Index AuthorizationPolicy by namespace/labels\n7. **initTelemetry()** - Process Telemetry resources for observability config\n8. **initProxyConfigs()** - Load ProxyConfig resources\n9. **initWasmPlugins()** - Index WASM plugins by namespace\n10. **initEnvoyFilters()** - Index EnvoyFilters for proxy patching\n11. **initGateways()** - Index Istio Gateway resources\n12. **initAmbient()** - Initialize ambient mesh data structures\n13. **initSidecarScopes()** - Compute per-proxy visibility (must be last)\n\n#### Incremental Update (`updateContext()`)\n\nReuses old indexes for unchanged config types:\n\n- Detects what changed: `for conf := range pushReq.ConfigsUpdated`\n- Only rebuilds affected indexes (e.g., if VirtualService changed, rebuild virtualServiceIndex)\n- Copies unchanged indexes from old context\n- Helps with performance when changes are localized\n\n### Config Translation: From Istio to Envoy\n\nGenerators translate Istio config to Envoy via `ConfigGenerator` interface. Key generators:\n\n#### CDS Generator (`pilot/pkg/xds/cds.go`)\n\nTranslates Services, VirtualServices, and DestinationRules \u2192 Envoy Clusters:\n\n```go\ntype CdsGenerator struct {\n    ConfigGenerator core.ConfigGenerator\n}\n\nfunc (c CdsGenerator) Generate(proxy, watched, req) (Resources, error) {\n    return c.ConfigGenerator.BuildClusters(proxy, req, watched.ResourceNames)\n}\n```\n\n**Filter:** Skips configs that don't impact clusters (e.g., Gateway, AuthorizationPolicy)\n\n#### RDS Generator (`pilot/pkg/xds/rds.go`)\n\nTranslates VirtualServices and DestinationRules \u2192 Envoy Routes:\n\n```go\nfunc (c RdsGenerator) Generate(proxy, watched, req) (Resources, error) {\n    return c.ConfigGenerator.BuildHTTPRoutes(proxy, req, watched.ResourceNames)\n}\n```\n\n**Filter:** Skips configs that don't impact routes (e.g., WorkloadEntry, RequestAuthentication)\n\n#### LDS Generator (`pilot/pkg/xds/lds.go`)\n\nTranslates Sidecars, Gateways, and VirtualServices \u2192 Envoy Listeners\n\n#### EDS Generator (`pilot/pkg/xds/eds.go`)\n\nTranslates ServiceInstances and Endpoints \u2192 Envoy Endpoints (load balancing destinations)\n\n### Translation Process\n\nFor each proxy, generators follow this pattern:\n\n1. **Read Config:** Access PushContext indexes (VirtualServices, DestinationRules, etc.)\n2. **Filter by Scope:** Apply sidecar scope, namespace, RBAC rules\n3. **Merge Config:** Combine multiple resources (e.g., merged DestinationRules)\n4. **Transform:** Convert Istio semantics to Envoy equivalents\n   - VirtualService routes \u2192 Envoy RouteConfiguration\n   - DestinationRule subsets \u2192 Envoy Cluster subsets with labels\n   - ServiceEntry \u2192 Envoy Cluster with static/DNS endpoints\n5. **Apply Patches:** Merge EnvoyFilter patches\n6. **Cache:** Store computed result keyed by (proxy, resource-type, push-version)\n\n### Sidecar Scopes\n\n**Critical for scalability:** Sidecar resources define which services each proxy can reach, enabling:\n\n- Per-proxy visibility filtering (only send needed clusters/routes)\n- Namespace-level isolation and multitenancy\n- Waypoint/gateway specific configurations\n\nComputed in `initSidecarScopes()` and cached on the proxy:\n\n```go\nproxy.SidecarScope = ps.GetSidecarScope(proxy, ns)\n```\n\n---\n\n## 4. Service Registry and Multi-Cluster Support\n\n**Location:** `pilot/pkg/model/service.go`, `pilot/pkg/model/controller.go`\n\nThe service registry layer abstracts away platform specifics (Kubernetes, VMs, external services) and provides a unified view of services in the mesh.\n\n### Service Model\n\n```go\ntype Service struct {\n    Hostname host.Name  // FQDN (e.g., \"svc.default.svc.cluster.local\")\n    Ports PortList  // Listening ports\n\n    Attributes ServiceAttributes\n        \u251c\u2500 Name string  // Short name\n        \u251c\u2500 Namespace string  // Kubernetes namespace\n        \u251c\u2500 Labels map[string]string  // User labels\n        \u251c\u2500 ExportTo visibility.Instance  // Who can see this service\n        \u2514\u2500 TrafficDistribution string  // Locality-aware LB policy\n\n    ClusterVIPs AddressMap  // VIP per cluster (multi-cluster support)\n    Resolution Resolution  // ClientSideLB, DNSLB, Passthrough, etc.\n    MeshExternal bool  // True if external to mesh (ServiceEntry)\n}\n```\n\nEach service can have multiple endpoints (IstioEndpoints) across clusters:\n\n```go\ntype IstioEndpoint struct {\n    Address string  // Pod IP or external IP\n    Port int  // Service port\n    Network string  // Cluster network\n    Labels labels.Instance  // Pod labels (subset selection)\n    Locality *core.Locality  // Zone/region\n}\n```\n\n### Controller Interface\n\n**Location:** `pilot/pkg/model/controller.go`\n\n```go\ntype Controller interface {\n    AppendServiceHandler(f ServiceHandler)  // Subscribe to service changes\n    AppendWorkloadHandler(f func(*WorkloadInstance, Event))  // Subscribe to workload changes\n    Run(stop <-chan struct{})  // Start the controller\n    HasSynced() bool  // Ready to serve requests\n}\n\ntype ServiceHandler func(prev, curr *Service, event Event)\n```\n\nControllers watch Kubernetes/VM resources and notify Pilot when:\n- **EventAdd:** New service created\n- **EventUpdate:** Service modified (ports, labels, endpoints)\n- **EventDelete:** Service removed\n\n### Aggregated Registry Pattern\n\nPilot supports multiple registries (per cluster in multi-cluster, or multiple connectors):\n\n```go\ntype AggregateController interface {\n    Controller\n    AppendServiceHandlerForCluster(clusterID, handler)\n    UnRegisterHandlersForCluster(clusterID)\n}\n```\n\nWhen a service update arrives from any cluster:\n\n1. **Handler fires** (e.g., Kubernetes controller detects endpoint change)\n2. **EDSUpdate or SvcUpdate** called on XDSUpdater (DiscoveryServer implements this)\n3. **PushRequest generated** with trigger reason (EndpointUpdate, ServiceUpdate, etc.)\n4. **Debouncer receives** the request\n5. **Affected proxies** enqueued for push\n\n### Multi-Cluster Data Flow\n\nIn a multi-cluster mesh:\n\n1. **Per-cluster Pilot instances** run in each cluster\n2. **Remote secret watchers** connect to remote API servers\n3. **Services aggregated** from all clusters into unified ServiceIndex\n4. **ClusterVIPs** stored per cluster (same FQDN, different VIPs in each cluster)\n5. **Endpoints aggregated** across clusters, sorted by network locality\n6. **Proxies in one cluster** receive routes to services in all clusters\n\nExample endpoint distribution:\n\n```\nService: productpage.default.svc.cluster.local\n\u251c\u2500 Cluster A (network: network-a)\n\u2502  \u2514\u2500 Pod 10.1.1.1:9080 (zone: us-west-1a)\n\u2502  \u2514\u2500 Pod 10.1.2.1:9080 (zone: us-west-1b)\n\u251c\u2500 Cluster B (network: network-b)\n\u2502  \u2514\u2500 Pod 10.2.1.1:9080 (zone: us-east-1a)\n```\n\nWhen a proxy in Cluster A requests endpoints:\n\n1. Local endpoints prioritized (same network)\n2. Remote endpoints included with gateway (cross-cluster LB traffic)\n3. Network labels used for traffic policies\n\n### Service Discovery Sources\n\n#### Kubernetes Registries\n\n- **K8s Services** \u2192 Service.Hostname, VIP\n- **K8s Endpoints** \u2192 IstioEndpoint list with pod labels/IPs\n- **K8s Pods** \u2192 Locality (zone labels), workload identity\n- **Labels** \u2192 Subset selection in DestinationRule\n\n#### ServiceEntry Resources\n\nCustom services (external, VMs):\n\n```yaml\napiVersion: networking.istio.io/v1alpha3\nkind: ServiceEntry\nmetadata:\n  name: external-api\nspec:\n  hosts:\n  - api.external.com\n  ports:\n  - number: 443\n    name: https\n  location: MESH_EXTERNAL\n  endpoints:\n  - address: 192.0.2.1  # External IP\n    ports:\n      https: 443\n```\n\nTreated like any other service, but endpoints are static/DNS.\n\n#### Workload Entry Resources\n\nVMs or external hosts:\n\n```yaml\napiVersion: networking.istio.io/v1alpha3\nkind: WorkloadEntry\nmetadata:\n  name: vm-1\n  namespace: default\nspec:\n  address: 192.0.2.100\n  labels:\n    app: database\n    version: v1\n```\n\nMerged into service endpoints, participate in Sidecar and DestinationRule scoping.\n\n### Service Registry Triggers\n\nWhen endpoints change, `EDSUpdate` enqueues only affected proxies:\n\n```go\nfunc (s *DiscoveryServer) EDSUpdate(shard, hostname, namespace, endpoints)\n```\n\nThis avoids full pushes\u2014only EDS (endpoint list) is recomputed:\n\n- **Trigger:** Pod scaled up/down, health changed\n- **Reason:** EndpointUpdate\n- **Full:** false (incremental update)\n- **ConfigsUpdated:** empty (means all proxies potentially affected, but only EDS recomputed)\n\nThis keeps endpoint changes fast and lightweight.\n\n---\n\n## Error Handling\n\n### Connection Errors\n\n**Scenarios:**\n- Proxy disconnects unexpectedly \u2192 `closeConnection()` removes from `adsClients`\n- Invalid metadata \u2192 return error, reject connection\n- Authorization fails \u2192 return error, deny access\n\n**Recovery:** Proxy reconnects with backoff; no state loss (stateless design)\n\n### Push Errors\n\n**Scenarios:**\n- Generator panics \u2192 recover and log error\n- Cache miss (shouldn't happen) \u2192 regenerate on the fly\n- Network error sending response \u2192 connection drops, proxy reconnects\n\n**Tracking:** Errors recorded in `PushContext.ProxyStatus[metricName]` for debugging\n\n### Config Errors\n\n**Scenarios:**\n- Invalid VirtualService \u2192 Validation errors logged but push continues\n- Circular service references \u2192 Detection and logging\n- Missing DestinationRule \u2192 Graceful fallback to default behavior\n\n**Mechanism:** Dedicated validation phase before push; errors recorded and exposed on debug endpoint\n\n---\n\n## Extension Points\n\n### Custom Generators\n\nOverride default resource generation:\n\n```go\nserver.Generators[\"my-custom\"] = &MyCustomGenerator{...}\n```\n\nProxy metadata `Generator: \"my-custom\"` triggers custom generator.\n\n### Custom Controllers\n\nAdd new service discovery sources:\n\n```go\nenv.ServiceDiscovery.(*aggregate.Controller).AddRegistry(myRegistry)\n```\n\nImplement `Controller` interface, register handlers.\n\n### ProxyNeedsPush Filter\n\nSkip pushes for proxies that don't need updates:\n\n```go\nserver.ProxyNeedsPush = func(proxy *model.Proxy, req *model.PushRequest) (*model.PushRequest, bool) {\n    // Custom logic: can we skip this push?\n    if req.Full && !proxy.NeedsFull() {\n        return req, false  // Skip\n    }\n    return req, true  // Send\n}\n```\n\n### EnvoyFilter Integration\n\nPatch generated Envoy config per proxy:\n\n```yaml\napiVersion: networking.istio.io/v1alpha3\nkind: EnvoyFilter\nmetadata:\n  name: auth-patch\nspec:\n  workloadSelector:\n    labels:\n      app: frontend\n  configPatches:\n  - applyTo: LISTENER\n    patch:\n      operation: MERGE\n      value:\n        # Merge custom listener config\n```\n\n---\n\n## Data Flow Example: Service Creation to Proxy Update\n\n### Scenario\nA new Kubernetes Service `shipping.default` is created with 2 pods.\n\n### Flow\n\n```\n1. Kubernetes API Server\n   \u2514\u2500 Event: Service \"shipping\" created\n\n2. K8s Service Registry Watcher\n   \u2514\u2500 Handler: onServiceCreate()\n\n3. XDSUpdater.SvcUpdate()\n   \u251c\u2500 Reason: ServiceUpdate\n   \u2514\u2500 \u2192 DiscoveryServer.ConfigUpdate()\n\n4. DiscoveryServer.ConfigUpdate()\n   \u251c\u2500 Increment InboundUpdates counter\n   \u251c\u2500 Send to pushChannel\n   \u2514\u2500 (May be debounced)\n\n5. handleUpdates() (debounce goroutine)\n   \u251c\u2500 Wait: DebounceAfter time since last event\n   \u251c\u2500 Call: Push(req)\n   \u2514\u2500 Increment CommittedUpdates counter\n\n6. DiscoveryServer.Push()\n   \u251c\u2500 Is Full push? YES (service is global config)\n   \u251c\u2500 Call: initPushContext()\n   \u2502  \u251c\u2500 NewPushContext created\n   \u2502  \u251c\u2500 InitContext() called:\n   \u2502  \u2502  \u251c\u2500 createNewContext() (or updateContext if incremental)\n   \u2502  \u2502  \u251c\u2500 initServiceRegistry() loads Services (including new \"shipping\")\n   \u2502  \u2502  \u251c\u2500 initDestinationRules()\n   \u2502  \u2502  \u251c\u2500 initVirtualServices()\n   \u2502  \u2502  \u2514\u2500 initSidecarScopes() computes per-proxy visibility\n   \u2502  \u2514\u2500 Store in Env.pushContext\n   \u251c\u2500 dropCacheForRequest() clear old xDS cache\n   \u2514\u2500 Call: AdsPushAll(req)\n\n7. AdsPushAll()\n   \u251c\u2500 For each proxy in adsClients:\n   \u2502  \u2514\u2500 pushQueue.Enqueue(proxy, req)\n   \u2514\u2500 Proxies queued\n\n8. sendPushes() (push worker goroutine)\n   \u251c\u2500 Acquire concurrentPushLimit semaphore\n   \u251c\u2500 Dequeue proxy from pushQueue\n   \u251c\u2500 Call: pushConnection(proxy, pushReq)\n   \u2502  \u251c\u2500 For each watched resource type (CDS, RDS, EDS):\n   \u2502  \u2502  \u251c\u2500 Call: CdsGenerator.Generate(proxy, req)\n   \u2502  \u2502  \u2502  \u251c\u2500 Access: ps.ServiceIndex (includes new \"shipping\")\n   \u2502  \u2502  \u2502  \u251c\u2500 Filter by proxy SidecarScope (can proxy reach \"shipping\"?)\n   \u2502  \u2502  \u2502  \u251c\u2500 Transform: Service \u2192 Envoy Cluster\n   \u2502  \u2502  \u2502  \u251c\u2500 Cache result\n   \u2502  \u2502  \u2502  \u2514\u2500 Return Cluster resources\n   \u2502  \u2502  \u2514\u2500 Build response\n   \u2502  \u2514\u2500 Send DiscoveryResponse via gRPC\n   \u251c\u2500 Queue marks done\n   \u2514\u2500 Release semaphore\n\n9. Envoy Proxy Receives\n   \u251c\u2500 Response: clusters=[..., {name: \"outbound|80||shipping.default.svc.cluster.local\", ...}]\n   \u251c\u2500 Version: \"2024-02-21T14:30:45Z/12345\"\n   \u251c\u2500 Nonce: \"uuid-xyz\"\n   \u2514\u2500 Proxy ACKs with same nonce\n\n10. Proxy Configuration Updated\n    \u251c\u2500 New cluster routing to \"shipping.default\" endpoints\n    \u251c\u2500 Future requests sent to shipping pods\n    \u2514\u2500 No manual intervention needed\n```\n\n---\n\n## Key Performance Characteristics\n\n### Scalability Features\n\n1. **Incremental Pushes:** Only affected proxies enqueued (via SidecarScope filtering)\n2. **Debouncing:** Multiple config changes merged into single push\n3. **Concurrent Push Limiting:** Prevents thundering herd, steady resource usage\n4. **Request Rate Limiting:** Per-connection rate limiter on new xDS requests\n5. **Caching:** xDS resources cached by (proxy, resource-type, version)\n6. **Index Structures:** ServiceIndex, virtualServiceIndex, etc. enable O(1) lookups\n\n### Timing\n\n- **Debounce latency:** 100ms\u201310s (configurable)\n- **Push time:** Typically < 1s for 100-1000 proxies\n- **Connection init:** ~100ms (includes service target computation)\n\n---\n\n## Relevant Source Files\n\n### Core Components\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/discovery.go` \u2014 DiscoveryServer, push coordination, debouncing\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/ads.go` \u2014 ADS stream handler, Connection, request processing\n- `pilot/pkg/model/push_context.go` \u2014 PushContext, config initialization, indexes\n- `pilot/pkg/model/context.go` \u2014 Environment (push context holder)\n\n### Generators & Translation\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/cds.go` \u2014 Cluster Discovery Service generator\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/lds.go` \u2014 Listener Discovery Service generator\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/rds.go` \u2014 Route Discovery Service generator\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/eds.go` \u2014 Endpoint Discovery Service generator\n- `pilot/pkg/networking/core/` \u2014 ConfigGenerator (main translation logic)\n\n### Service Registry & Discovery\n- `pilot/pkg/model/service.go` \u2014 Service, ServiceInstance, Resolution types\n- `pilot/pkg/model/controller.go` \u2014 Controller interface, event model\n- `pilot/pkg/serviceregistry/` \u2014 Kubernetes controller implementation\n\n### Queue & Concurrency\n- `pilot/pkg/xds/pushqueue.go` \u2014 PushQueue, proxy push ordering\n\n### Configuration Models\n- `pilot/pkg/model/destination_rule.go` \u2014 DestinationRule handling\n- `pilot/pkg/model/virtualservice.go` \u2014 VirtualService handling\n- `pilot/pkg/model/sidecar.go` \u2014 SidecarScope computation\n- `pilot/pkg/model/authentication.go` \u2014 AuthN/AuthZ policy models\n\n### Multi-Cluster\n- `pilot/pkg/model/network.go` \u2014 Network topology for multi-cluster\n- Cluster registry aggregation in ServiceDiscovery\n\n---\n\n## Conclusion\n\nPilot's Discovery Service achieves high performance and scalability through:\n\n1. **Separation of concerns:** DiscoveryServer handles gRPC; PushContext holds config snapshot; Generators handle translation\n2. **Smart filtering:** SidecarScope limits what each proxy needs; incremental pushes reduce work\n3. **Debouncing & rate limiting:** Prevents thrashing when many config changes occur\n4. **Pluggable architecture:** Custom generators, controllers, and filters enable extensions\n5. **Stateless design:** Proxies reconnect without data loss; connection state rebuilt from config\n\nThe architecture elegantly scales to thousands of proxies and supports advanced features like multi-cluster, ambient mesh, and traffic management with minimal manual tuning.\n",

# Istio Pilot Discovery Service Architecture

## Overview

The Pilot Discovery Service is the heart of Istio's configuration distribution system. It serves xDS (Envoy Discovery Service) resources to all proxies in the mesh, translating Istio's high-level networking configuration (VirtualServices, DestinationRules, etc.) into Envoy-native resources (Clusters, Routes, Listeners, Endpoints) that proxies understand natively.

This document explains the architecture of Pilot's discovery subsystem—how it discovers services, translates configuration, manages proxy connections, and coordinates pushes across the fleet.

---

## Component Responsibilities

### 1. DiscoveryServer: The xDS gRPC Server

**Location:** `pilot/pkg/xds/discovery.go`

The `DiscoveryServer` struct is the central gRPC server implementing Envoy's xDS v3 APIs. It is responsible for:

- **Registering the gRPC service:** Implements `AggregatedDiscoveryService` interface
- **Accepting proxy connections:** Handles new xDS streams from Envoy proxies
- **Managing active connections:** Maintains a map of connected proxies via `adsClients`
- **Coordinating configuration pushes:** Orchestrates when and how config updates are sent to proxies
- **Debouncing and rate limiting:** Prevents thundering herd of configuration updates

#### Key Fields

```go
type DiscoveryServer struct {
    Env *model.Environment                    // Access to mesh state, services, config
    Generators map[string]model.XdsResourceGenerator  // Pluggable generators per resource type
    ProxyNeedsPush func(proxy, req) (*PushRequest, bool)  // Filter unnecessary pushes

    // Connection management
    adsClients map[string]*Connection        // Active proxy connections
    adsClientsMutex sync.RWMutex             // Protects adsClients

    
... (truncated)
